 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. is furnishing this Current Report on Form 8-K in order to furnish to the Securities and Exchange Commission a press
release that we will issue on February&nbsp;21, 2012 (the &#147;Press Release&#148;). The Press Release will disclose information regarding our results of operations for the three months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2012 and our financial
condition as of January&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release provides information regarding certain financial measures that may
be considered non-GAAP financial measures (each, a &#147;Non-GAAP Measure&#148;) under the rules of the Securities and Exchange Commission. Among those Non-GAAP Measures are: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Financial measures presented on a constant currency basis (each, a &#147;Constant Currency Measure&#148;). Constant Currency Measures are calculated by
translating the results of our Walmart International operating segment (&#147;Walmart International&#148;) for a fiscal period in the local currencies in which Walmart International operates into U.S. dollars using the currency exchange rates used
to translate the similar results of Walmart International for the prior year comparable period into U.S. dollars to report those prior period results in our consolidated financial statements. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Financial measures (the &#147;Adjusted Financial Measures&#148;) relating to our consolidated net sales and Walmart International&#146;s consolidated
net sales for certain periods and certain period-over-period increases in our consolidated net sales and consolidated operating income and Walmart International&#146;s net sales and operating income, in each case, presented on a constant currency
basis and excluding the results of the Netto stores in the United Kingdom and of Massmart Holdings Ltd. in South Africa, the acquisitions of which were completed during the three months ended July&nbsp;31, 2011 (the &#147;Acquisitions&#148;).
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our total U.S. comparable store sales and the comparable club sales of our Sam&#146;s Club operating segment (&#147;Sam&#146;s Club&#148;) for the
thirteen-week and fifty-two-week periods ended January&nbsp;27, 2012 and January&nbsp;28, 2011 calculated excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for such periods. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The net sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2012, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for that
three-month period and that fiscal year, and the percentage increase in the net sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2012, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the three
months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2012, over the net sales and operating income, respectively, of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2011, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the three
months and fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2011. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release provides information that reconciles
each of these Non-GAAP Measures to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our management believes that the
presentation of the Non-GAAP Measures discussed above provides useful information to investors regarding our financial condition and results of operations as to the periods for which they are presented for the following reasons: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We are required to translate Walmart International&#146;s operating results as stated in local currencies into U.S. dollars to report our consolidated
results of operations in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles as in effect in the United States. Period-over-period comparisons of our consolidated results of operations can be affected by the differences between currency
exchange rates in the prior fiscal period to which the comparison is made and the currency exchange rates in the current fiscal period as reflected in our consolidated results of operations reported in U.S. dollars, making an investor&#146;s
assessment of the underlying performance of Walmart International and its effect on total company underlying performance for the current fiscal period more difficult. The presentation of the Constant Currency Measures permits investors to understand
important aspects of Walmart International&#146;s underlying performance in the current fiscal period without the effect of any period-to-period fluctuations in applicable currency exchange rates and how that performance would have affected our
consolidated results of operations in the current fiscal period and in period-over-period comparisons had currency exchange rates remained constant since the comparable prior year period. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The presentation of the Adjusted Financial Measures permits investors to understand the combined effects of currency exchange rate translations and the
Acquisitions on our consolidated net sales and Walmart International&#146;s net sales and on the period-over-period increases in our consolidated net sales and consolidated operating income and Walmart International&#146;s net sales and operating
income, in each case for the periods as to </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
which the Adjusted Financial Measures are presented, and what our financial performance as reflected by those measures would have been for the periods for which the Adjusted Financial Measures
are presented without the combined effects of currency exchange rate translations and the Acquisitions. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The presentation of our total U.S. comparable store sales, Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s comparable club sales, the net sales and operating income of
Sam&#146;s Club and the period-over-period percentage increase in the net sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club, calculated, in each case, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club, permits investors to understand the effect of such fuel
sales, which are affected by the volatility of fuel prices, on our total U.S. comparable store sales, on Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s comparable club sales and on Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s net sales and operating income for the periods presented.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Exhibit 99.1&#151;A copy of the Press Release being furnished pursuant to the foregoing Item&nbsp;2.02 is included herewith as Exhibit
99.1. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Walmart U.S. delivers positive traffic and positive comp sales in Q4 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Walmart reported fourth quarter diluted earnings per share from continuing operations (EPS) of $1.51, which included net benefits of approximately
$0.07 from certain tax matters and real estate transactions. The company&#146;s EPS guidance for the quarter of $1.42 to $1.48 did not include these net benefits. This EPS compared to $1.41 last year, which included net tax benefits of approximately
$0.07. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>BENTONVILLE, Ark., Feb. 21, 2012</B> &#151; Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (NYSE: WMT) today reported financial
results for the fourth quarter and full year ended Jan. 31, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net sales for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2012 were $122.3 billion, an
increase of 5.8 percent from $115.6 billion in last year&#146;s fourth quarter. Net sales for the quarter included $2.4 billion of positive impact from the acquisitions of the Netto stores in the U.K. and Massmart in South Africa. Net sales included
approximately $1.0 billion of negative impact from currency exchange rates. Before acquisitions, and on a constant currency basis, net sales grew 4.5 percent to $120.9 billion. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income from continuing operations attributable to Walmart for the quarter was $5.2 billion, up 3.4 percent from $5.0 billion last year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Diluted earnings per share from continuing operations attributable to Walmart (EPS) for the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2012 were $1.51. EPS for the quarter benefited $0.07 from the following items:
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A net pre-tax benefit of $68 million related to a real estate gain and store closure transactions in Brazil; and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A benefit of $187 million from income tax expense being lower than anticipated for the quarter. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The company&#146;s EPS guidance for the quarter of $1.42 to $1.48 did not include these net benefits. In comparison, EPS for the fourth quarter of last
fiscal year was $1.41, which included a net tax benefit of $243 million, or approximately $0.07 per share. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U></U></B><U>Fiscal 2012
results<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consolidated net sales for the full fiscal year were $443.9 billion, an increase of 5.9 percent over fiscal year 2011. Net
sales included approximately $4.7 billion of positive impact from acquisitions and approximately $4.0 billion of positive impact from currency exchange rates. Before acquisitions, and on a constant currency basis, net sales grew 3.9 percent to
$435.1 billion. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income from continuing operations attributable to Walmart was $15.8 billion, a 2.7 percent increase from $15.4 billion last
year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For fiscal year 2012, EPS was $4.54 versus last year&#146;s EPS of $4.18. This fiscal year included net benefits of certain items of
$0.05 compared to $0.11 last year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U></U></B><U>Earnings performance<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We are pleased with Walmart&#146;s earnings performance for both the fourth quarter and the full year,&#148; said Mike Duke, Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. president and chief executive officer. &#147;Today,
every segment of our business is stronger than it was a year ago, and we&#146;re in a great position for fiscal year 2013.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Duke
recognized the progress Walmart U.S. made during the quarter. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Walmart U.S. reported positive comps of 1.5 percent for the fourth
quarter including positive comp traffic. This is now the second consecutive quarter of positive comp sales,&#148; he said. &#147;Our price leadership is making a difference across the United States, as many families are settling into a new normal.
Core customers remain cautious about their finances, and they rely on Walmart&#146;s EDLP promise to help them manage through today&#146;s economic challenges.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Duke also recognized the solid full year results of Walmart International and Sam&#146;s Club. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Walmart International delivered strong growth through both comp store sales and a record number of new
units, including the acquisitions of Netto and Massmart,&#148; said Duke. &#147;The leadership teams are focused on improving profitability, and our &#145;Powered by Walmart&#146; initiatives will strengthen productivity and reduce expenses in our
markets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Sam&#146;s Club comp sales have been consistently strong throughout the year, and we expect this momentum to continue in
fiscal year 2013,&#148; Duke said. &#147;Operational efficiencies contributed to expense leverage and improved member experience. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:0px;"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Our company leveraged expenses for both the quarter and the full year,&#148; said Duke. &#147;In fact, Walmart has now leveraged operating expenses for two consecutive years. We have a relentless
focus on the productivity loop to drive down costs and pass those savings on to customers. And as I look forward to our
50</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">th</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> anniversary this year, I see tremendous opportunities
still ahead for our company and our shareholders.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U></U></B><U>Strong returns<B> </B></U></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During the fourth quarter, the company repurchased approximately 22.9&nbsp;million shares for $1.3 billion, bringing the full year repurchases to
115.3&nbsp;million shares for $6.3 billion. In addition, the company paid $1.2 billion and $5.0 billion in dividends for the quarter and year, respectively. For the year, Walmart returned $11.3 billion to shareholders through dividends and share
repurchases. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:0px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart ended the year with free cash flow of $10.7 billion</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><I>1</I></SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">, compared to $10.9 billion</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><I>1</I></SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> in the prior year. The modest decline in free cash flow was
primarily due to capital expenditures outpacing the growth in net cash from operating activities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:0px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Return on investment
(ROI) for the year ended Jan. 31, 2012 was 18.6 percent</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><I>1</I></SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">, compared to 19.2 percent</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"><I>1</I></SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> for the prior year. ROI was impacted adversely by additional investments in property, plant and equipment (PP&amp;E), Global eCommerce, and higher inventories, as well as price investment ahead of full
realization of productivity improvements. In future quarters, productivity gains are expected to more closely align with price investments. Additionally, to a lesser degree, ROI was positively impacted by currency gains, but offset by acquisitions.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U></U></B><U>EPS guidance<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Our operating segments are well positioned for this fiscal year. Taking into consideration the current economy and operating environment, we expect first quarter fiscal 2013 diluted earnings per
share from continuing operations attributable to Walmart to range between $1.01 and $1.06,&#148; said Charles Holley, executive vice president and chief financial officer. &#147;In fiscal year 2012, we reported EPS of $0.98 for the first quarter,
which included a $0.01 net benefit from multiple items. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Looking at our goals for the full fiscal year, we expect continued growth in
sales and earnings. We also plan to deliver strong free cash flow,&#148; Holley said. &#147;For the full year, we expect diluted earnings per share from continuing operations attributable to Walmart to range between $4.72 and $4.92. This compares to
the EPS of $4.54, which we reported today and included $0.05 of net benefits from certain items. All EPS guidance assumes that currency rates remain at today&#146;s levels and take into account our forecast for the fiscal 2013 effective tax rate to
range between 32.5 percent and 33.5 percent.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000;width:10%">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;All three Walmart U.S. geographic units delivered positive comps, reinforcing that our plan is working and
resonating with customers. Our stores have greater price leadership, broader assortment, and improved on-shelf availability. The combination of these factors contributed to positive traffic,&#148; said Bill Simon, Walmart U.S. president and CEO.
&#147;We invested in price in the fourth quarter and will continue to do so through this fiscal year, so we can pass savings on to customers. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Heading into this fiscal year, we will build on our fourth quarter results and drive continued improvement for our customers and
shareholders,&#148; said Simon. &#147;We are forecasting Walmart U.S. comp sales for the 13-week period from Jan. 28 through Apr. 27 to range from flat to positive two percent.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Sam&#146;s Club net sales were strong, and we managed our gross margin rate well in a competitive and inflationary pricing environment in the fourth quarter,&#148; said Rosalind Brewer, Sam&#146;s
Club president and CEO. &#147;Our entire organization is motivated to continue our top line and comp sales momentum. Our members continue to respond to key merchandising initiatives, and we expect comp club sales, without fuel, for the 13-week
period from Jan. 28 through Apr. 27 to increase three to five percent.&#148; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart U.S. and Sam&#146;s Club will report comparable sales for the 13-week period ending Apr. 27
on&nbsp;May&nbsp;17 when the company reports first quarter results. Last fiscal year for the first 13-week period, Walmart U.S. reported a comparable store decline of 1.1 percent, and Sam&#146;s Club increased comparable club sales, without fuel,
4.2 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For fiscal year 2013, the first quarter&#146;s 4-5-4 comparable sales will not be impacted by the additional leap-year day of
Feb. 29. Walmart will report comparable store sales for fiscal year 2013 on a 53-week basis, with 4-5-5 reporting for the fourth quarter. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Notes </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Constant currency results
are calculated by translating current year results using prior year exchange rates. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">After this earnings release has been furnished to the
Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC), a pre-recorded call offering additional comments on the quarter will be available to all investors. Callers may listen to this call by dialing 800-778-6902, or 585-219-6420 outside the U.S. and Canada.
Information included in this release, including reconciliations, and the pre-recorded phone call are available in the investor information area on the company&#146;s website at <U>www.walmartstores.com/investors</U>. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (NYSE: WMT) serves customers and members more than 200&nbsp;million times per week at 10,130 retail units under 69 different
banners in 27 countries. With fiscal year 2012 sales of approximately $444 billion, Walmart employs more than 2&nbsp;million associates worldwide. Walmart continues to be a leader in sustainability, corporate philanthropy and employment opportunity.
Additional information about Walmart can be found by visiting <U>http://www.walmartstores.com</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Forward Looking Statements

continuing operations attributable to Walmart for the fiscal quarter to end April&nbsp;30, 2012 and the fiscal year to end Jan. 31, 2013 (and a statement of certain assumptions underlying such forecasts), management&#146;s forecasts of the
company&#146;s effective tax rate for the fiscal year to end January&nbsp;31, 2013, the comparable store sales of the Walmart U.S. segment of the company and the comparable club sales, excluding fuel, of the Sam&#146;s Club segment of the company
for the 13-week period from Jan. 28, 2012 through Apr. 27, 2012, and management&#146;s expectations regarding productivity gains more closely aligning with price investments in future quarters, continued growth in Walmart&#146;s sales and earnings,
Walmart&#146;s plan to deliver strong free cash flow, the Walmart U.S. operating segment continuing to invest in price, building on its results for the quarter ended Jan. 31, 2012 and driving continued improvement, &#147;Powered by Walmart&#148;
initiatives strengthening productivity and reducing expenses within the Walmart International operating segment and Walmart&#146;s Sam&#146;s Club operating segment comp sales momentum continuing in fiscal year 2013 that the company believes are

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Reconciliations of and Other Information regarding Non-GAAP Financial Measures </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(Unaudited) </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>(In millions, except per share data) </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following information provides reconciliations of certain non-GAAP financial measures presented in the press release to which this reconciliation is attached to the most directly comparable financial
measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). The company has provided the non-GAAP financial information presented in the press release, which is not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as information supplemental and in addition to the financial measures presented in the press release that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. Such non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered superior
to, as a substitute for, or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. The non-GAAP financial measures in the press release may differ from similar measures used by
other companies. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Free Cash Flow </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define free cash flow as net cash provided by operating activities in a period minus payments for property and equipment made in that period. Free cash flow was $10.7 billion and $10.9 billion for the
fiscal years ended Jan. 31, 2012 and 2011, respectively. The modest decline in free cash flow was primarily due to capital expenditures outpacing the growth in net cash from operating activities. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow is considered a non-GAAP financial measure under the SEC&#146;s rules. Management believes, however, that free cash flow, which measures
our ability to generate additional cash from our business operations, is an important financial measure for use in evaluating the company&#146;s financial performance. Free cash flow should be considered in addition to, rather than as a substitute
for, income from continuing operations as a measure of our performance and net cash provided by operating activities as a measure of our liquidity. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Additionally, our definition of free cash flow is limited, in that it does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures due to the fact that the measure does not deduct the
payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments made for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire
statements of cash flows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Although other companies report their free cash flow, numerous methods may exist for calculating a company&#146;s
free cash flow. As a result, the method used by our management to calculate free cash flow may differ from the methods other companies use to calculate their free cash flow. We urge you to understand the methods used by another company to calculate
its free cash flow before comparing our free cash flow to that of such other company. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following table sets forth a reconciliation of free
cash flow, a non-GAAP financial measure, to net cash provided by operating activities, a GAAP measure, which we believe to be the GAAP financial measure most directly comparable to free cash flow, for the fiscal years ended Jan. 31, 2012 and 2011,
as well as information regarding net cash used in investing activities and net cash used in financing activities in those periods. </FONT></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Calculation of Return on Investment and Return on Assets </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Management believes return on investment (&#147;ROI&#148;) is a meaningful metric to share with investors because it helps investors assess how effectively Walmart is employing its assets. Trends in ROI
can fluctuate over time as management balances long-term potential strategic initiatives with any possible short-term impacts. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">ROI was 18.6
percent and 19.2 percent for the fiscal years ended Jan. 31, 2012 and 2011, respectively. ROI was impacted adversely by additional investments in property, plant and equipment (PP&amp;E), Global eCommerce, and higher inventories, as well as price
investment ahead of full realization of productivity improvements. In future quarters, productivity gains are expected to more closely align with price investments. Additionally, to a lesser degree, ROI was positively impacted by currency gains, but
offset by acquisitions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define ROI as adjusted operating income (operating income plus interest income, depreciation and amortization, and
rent expense) for the fiscal year divided by average invested capital during that period. We consider average invested capital to be the average of our beginning and ending total assets of continuing operations, plus accumulated depreciation and
amortization less accounts payable and accrued liabilities for that period, plus a rent factor equal to the rent for the fiscal year multiplied by a factor of eight. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">ROI is considered a non-GAAP financial measure under the SEC&#146;s rules. We consider return on assets (&#147;ROA&#148;) to be the financial measure computed in accordance with GAAP that is the most
directly comparable financial measure to ROI as we calculate that financial measure. ROI differs from ROA (which is income from continuing operations for the fiscal year or trailing twelve months divided by average total assets of continuing
operations for the period) because ROI: adjusts operating income to exclude certain expense items and adds interest income; adjusts total assets from continuing operations for the impact of accumulated depreciation and amortization, accounts payable
and accrued liabilities; and incorporates a factor of rent to arrive at total invested capital. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Although ROI is a standard financial metric,
numerous methods exist for calculating a company&#146;s ROI. As a result, the method used by Walmart&#146;s management to calculate ROI may differ from the methods other companies use to calculate their ROI. We urge you to understand the methods
used by another company to calculate its ROI before comparing our ROI to that of such other company. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">12 </FONT></P>



<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The calculation of ROI, along with reconciliation to the calculation of ROA, the most comparable GAAP
financial measurement, is as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Return on Investment and Return on Assets </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
